      <div class="sqs-layout sqs-grid-12 columns-12" data-type="page-section" id="page-section-5eb8245598232c36f5dc6594"><div class="row sqs-row"><div class="col sqs-col-12 span-12"><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1598543497110_23467"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"></p><h2 style="text-align:center;white-space:pre-wrap;">CONSERVATION INSPIRATION</h2><p class="sqsrte-large" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">As a Florida based company, we were inspired by the conservation efforts to protect our local coral reefs. Introduced illegally in the 1980s, Lionfish are known to wreck havoc along all Caribbean reefs. In fact, divers and local governments encourage you to hunt and eat them!  We wanted to take it a step further and have you hunt them and all their polluted minions in VR.<br><br>These ecosystems are under constant threat. It’s our hope our little game inspires you a little more about what goes on beneath the waves and why it’s important to protect them</p><h2 style="text-align:center;white-space:pre-wrap;">💙💧 </h2>
</div>



</div></div></div></div></div>
    </div>
  
  </div>
  
</section>

      <div class="sqs-layout sqs-grid-12 columns-12" data-type="page-section" id="page-section-60c784fdde72763ca76a38f7"><div class="row sqs-row"><div class="col sqs-col-5 span-5"><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-5333afb3a45962f41415"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h3 style="white-space:pre-wrap;">About Brave Lunch</h3><p class="sqsrte-small" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">BraveLunch is led by Emmy-nominated creative director David Andrade and technologist Mark Olson. Collectively, David and Mark have worked in the media industry for over 20 years in interactive experiences, theme park visuals and TV effects. Their credits include Universal Studios Orlando, Walt Disney Imagineering, Chimelong Ocean Kingdom, Amazon Studios' Man in the High Castle, Silicon Valley and Sesame Street.</p><p class="sqsrte-small" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">In 2017, David and his team were nominated for an Emmy and a Visual Effects Society award for their work on Man in the High Castle for CGI. In 2021, they were also nominated for a Themed Entertainment Association Award for their work on Universal Studios Orlando’s Bourne Stuntacular experience.</p><p class="sqsrte-small" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Based in Orlando, Florida and Calgary, Alberta, BraveLunch is a 15-person-strong animation and virtual reality studio working with some of the biggest names in entertainment. They announced their newest VR title, Blobkin Blaster, in 2020.</p><p class="" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"></p><h3 style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Contact</h3><p class="sqsrte-small" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Inquiries: hi@bravelunch.com</p><p class="sqsrte-small" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Twitter: https://twitter.com/bravelunch</p><p class="sqsrte-small" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Request a key: keys@bravelunch.com</p>
</div>



</div></div></div><div class="col sqs-col-1 span-1"><div class="sqs-block spacer-block sqs-block-spacer sized vsize-1" data-block-type="21" id="block-67abd39872f7ff6f5e57"><div class="sqs-block-content">&nbsp;</div></div></div><div class="col sqs-col-6 span-6"><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-154ccee8ca12adc4c7e4"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h2 style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Features</h2><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Classic Wave-shooter with multiple challenging enemies and waves.</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Mixed with real-time strategy building elements: cannons, decoys, supplies and more.</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">6 zones to battle in.</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Red-Tide mode, infinite, you-will-lose, combat against hoards of fish.</p></li></ul><h3 style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Release Date</h3><p style="margin-left:40px;white-space:pre-wrap;" class="">August 19, 2021</p><h3 style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Platforms</h3><p style="margin-left:40px;white-space:pre-wrap;" class="">PC Virtual Reality, currently supporting Oculus Quest with Link, Oculus Rift, &amp; Steam VR headsets (Vive, Cosmos, Index, Windows MR).</p>
</div>
